Example Response
API Documentation

kleio-server

The API is provided in a REST in REST and JSON-RPC versions. Not all functions are provided in both versions. In general functions that require sending structured input are exposed in JSON-RPC (tokens and users) while simple file fetching functions have only a REST version (exports, reports). A client would preferable use JSON-RPC and call REST to fetch files.

POST Invalidate_normal_user
http://localhost:8088/json/

Invalidate the normal user.

HEADERS
Content-Type
application/json

None

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{"jsonrpc": "2.0", 	"method": "users_invalidate", 
	"params": {
		"user":"tester",
		"token":"{{testadmintoken}}"
	},
	"id": {{request_id}}}
Example Request
  • Invalidate_normal_user
                                                
POST http://localhost:8088/json/

{"jsonrpc": "2.0", 	"method": "users_invalidate", 
	"params": {
		"user":"tester",
		"token":"7c689b969e59c0a244a5778b43cb7da135a90056"
	},
	"id": }

    },
    "id": {{request_id}}
}
Example Request
  • Generate Token (power user)
  • Generate Token (admin_user)
  • Generate Token (normal user)
  • Generate Token (limited user)
                                                
POST http://localhost:8089/json/
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "generate_token",
    "params": {
        "user": "power_user",
        "info": {
        	"comment": "An user able to translate, upload and delete files, and also create and remove directories",
            "api": [
                "sources",
                "kleioset",
                "files",
                "structures",
                "translations",
                "upload",
                "delete",
                "mkdir",
                "rmdir"
            ],
            "structures": "users/limited_user/stru",
            "sources": "sources/test_translations"
        },
        "token": "7c689b969e59c0a244a5778b43cb7da135a90056"
    },
    "id": 1
}

POST sources_get_file
http://{{endpoint}}/json/

Get a file. Obtains a link to download a file specified in the Path parameter

HEADERS
Content-Type
application/json

None

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "sources_get",
    "params": {
        "path": "paroquiais/casamentos/cas1714-1722.cli",
        "token": "{{remotetoken}}"
    },
    "id": 1987
}
Example Request
  • Sources Get File
                                                
POST http://localhost:8089/json/
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "sources_get",
    "params": {
        "path": "paroquiais/casamentos/cas1714-1722.cli",
        "token": "{{remotetoken}}"
    },
    "id": 1
}
Example Response
200 - OK 
                                                    
{
    "id": 1,
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "result": {
        "mime_type": "text/cli",
        "url": "/rest/sources/paroquiais/casamentos/cas1714-1722.cli"
    }
}
POST sources_get_files
http://{{endpoint}}/json/

Get the list of the source files in a Directory.

Params: * recurse: if yes, will recurse into subdirectories; if “no” or absent will return just the first level. * url: if yes then the urls for retrieving the files are returned.

HEADERS
Content-Type
application/json

None

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "sources_get",
    "params": {
        "path": "testes/sources/santaclara/svn/santaclara/ANTT",
        "recurse":"yes",
        "token": "{{tester_token}}"
    },
    "id": 1
}
Example Request
  • sources_get_files recurse
                                                
POST http://localhost:8089/json/
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "sources_get",
    "params": {
        "path": "paroquiais",
        "recurse":"yes",
        "token": ""
    },
    "id": 1
}
Example Response
200 - OK 
                                                    
{
    "id": 1,
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "result": [

POST translations_translate
http://{{endpoint}}/json/

Start a translation.

If path points to a directory translates files in the directory

Parameters:

  • structure: structure file to be used in the translation
  • echo : if yes the “rpt” file with include the source lines
  • recurse : descend into sub directories (default no)
  • status: filter files by translation status.
  • spawn : if yes the files are distributed to diferent workers and translated in parallell.
    if no (default) the files will be translated by a single worker, with the stru file being processed
    only once, at the start of the translation. In multi-user environment spawn=no should be used, so that
    different users can accesss free workers more easily.

HEADERS
Content-Type
application/json

None

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "translations_translate",
    "params": {
        "path": "testes/sources/perdoes/perdoesega/perdoes_ega.cli", 
        "spawn":"no",
        "token": "{{testusertoken}}"
    },
    "id": 1987
}
Example Request
  • translations_translate
                                                
POST http://localhost:8089/json/

{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "translations_translate",
    "params": {
        "path": "testes/sources/perdoes/perdoesega/perdoes_ega.cli", 
        "spawn":"no",
        "token": "{{testusertoken}}"
    },
    "id": 1987
}

GET versions_get_status_global
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/versions/status/global/?id=1234&recurse=yes

Gets information on the git repository associated with the sources.

The path after “versions” must start with a prefix that determines the type of information collected.

  • {Endpoint}/rest/versions/status/global[/path]
    • Gets an overview of the global status of the local branch, including divergence from origin and local change. The information is designed to provide an overview of what is going on in the remote and compare with local
      using logs and diff list.
    • It is possible to specify a local path after the prefix {Endpoint}/rest/version/status/global/baptisms/1650 but the result will always refer to the whole branch to which the directory is associated as if git status was issued at the root of the git repository.
  • {Endpoint}/rest/versions/remote/branches[/path]
    • Gets information on the branches of the remotes associated to the repository of Directory. Works with information of the last fetch.For each remote branch gathers the following information: Name, commits ahead of current branch, commits behind, info on remote (name, origin, url).

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

Prefer json output

PARAMS
id
1234

None

recurse
yes

recurse into subdirectories (yes/no)

Example Request
  • versions_get_status_global
                                                
GET http://localhost:8089/rest/versions/status/global/?id=1234&recurse=yes
POST versions_commit
http://{{endpoint}}/json/

Commit and Add files.

Commits files using the command:

git commit -m MESSAGE FILE1 FILE2 ...

Can also pre-add files using the command

git add FILE1 FILE2 FILE3

Note that the git commit command with explicit files as arguments will commit those files even if they are not stagged. Only files that are unkown to git must be added before commit and this can be done in a single call to this procedure by using the add_files parameter.

Parameters: * path: path to the directory (relative to the root directory associated with the token) * token: user token * gitparams: if present will add parameters after git commit, before “-m” * addfiles: paths of files to be added before commit. Files should be separated by spaces. This list is automaticlly added to the commit file list, so their are added and commited. * commitfiles:paths of files to be commited. Files should be separated by spaces. * commitmessage: message for the commit.

All file path are relative to the root directory of the git repository, as would be returned bit git status in the root directory. Check versions_get_status_global which provides the git status information in the workdir_status result.

Note that errors generated by the git command are returned as part of a result, in the fields: giterror, gitoutput and gitexitstatus, and not has json-rpc exceptions. If the git command executed then any result is considered a normal result, even if git specific errors were generated.

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "versions_commit",
    "params": {
        "path": "",
        "token": "{{remotetoken}}",
        "add_files": "README.md",
        "commit_files": "example.cli",
        "commit_message": "Cmmit through rpc"
    },
    "id": {{request_id}}
}
Example Request
  • versions_commit
                                                
POST http://localhost:8089/json/

{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "versions_commit",
    "params": {
        "path": "",
        "token": "{{remotetoken}}",
        "add_files": "README.md",
        "commit_files": "example.cli",
        "commit_message": "Cmmit through rpc"
    },
    "id": 
}
POST versions_set_user_info
http://{{endpoint}}/json/

Sets user name and email for commits.

If no user name and email are set before commit, git will generate an error.

Current user name and email and returned and part of versions_get_status_global call and also by the versions_get_user_info call.

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "versions_set_user_info",
    "params": {
        "path": "",
        "token": "{{remotetoken}}",
        "user_name": "Joaquim Carvalho",
        "user_email": "joaquim@uc.pt"
    },
    "id": {{request_id}}
}
Example Request

POST versions_reset
http://{{endpoint}}/json/

Retrieves user name and email currently configured for commits.

Returns ‘none’ when not defined.

See versions_set_user_info

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "versions_reset",
    "params": {
        "path": "",
        "token": "{{remotetoken}}",
        "reset_mode": "--hard",
        "commit_ref": "HEAD~1"
    },
    "id": {{request_id}}
}

GET sources_get_files
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/sources?id=1234&recurse=yes&url=yes

Get the list of the source files in a Directory.

Params: * recurse: if yes, will recurse into subdirectories; if “no” or absent will return just the first level. * url: if yes then the urls for retrieving the files are returned.

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

Prefer json output

PARAMS
id
1234

None

recurse
yes

None

url
yes

None

Example Request
  • sources_get_files text result
  • sources_get_files text url results
  • sources_get_files json results urls
                                                
GET http://localhost:8089/rest/sources/varia?id=1234&recurse=no
Example Response
200 - OK 
                                                    
varia/Devedores.cli
varia/auc_cartulario18.cli
varia/eleicoes1.cli
varia/misMesa.cli
varia/mp758-santiago-beduido.cli
varia/nommiz.cli
varia/sourecoimbrabispcoimbra_apontamentosd.cli
varia/vereacao.cli
varia/xpto_comuns_soure.kleio


                                                
                                                
GET http://localhost:8089/rest/sources/varia?id=1234&recurse=no&url=yes

POST translations_post
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/translations/testes/sources/perdoes/perdoesega/perdoes_ega.cli?id={{request_id}}&echo=no&spawn=yes&recurse=yes

Start a translation.

If path points to a directory translates files in the directory

Parameters:

  • structure: structure file to be used in the translation
  • echo : if yes the “rpt” file with include the source lines
  • recurse : descend into sub directories (default no)
  • status: filter files by translation status.
  • spawn : if yes the files are distributed to diferent workers and translated in parallell.
    if no (default) the files will be translated by a single worker, with the stru file being processed
    only once, at the start of the translation. In multi-user environment spawn=no should be used, so that
    different users can accesss free workers more easily.

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

None

PARAMS
id
{{request_id}}

None

echo
no

None

spawn
yes

None

recurse
yes

None

tstatus
T

None

Example Request
  • translations_post
                                                
POST http://localhost:8089/rest/translations/testes/sources/perdoes/perdoesega/perdoes_ega.cli?id=&echo=no&spawn=yes&recurse=yes
GET translations_get
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/translations/git?id={{request_id}}&recurse=yes

Returns the translation status of a source and various metadata

Info returned for every file (extension .cli or .kleio in the path)

  • name: the name of the file in File, without the path.
  • path: the full path to the file.

  • status: T,V,E,W,P,Q if more than one apply the priority is P

    • T=needs translation
    • V=valid translation (can be imported)
    • E=translated with errors
    • W=translated with warnings
    • Q=file is in queue for translation
    • P=file is currently being translated

  • modified: the time of last modification , as a float

  • modified_string: the formated time of last modification using format ‘%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S’
  • modified_rfc1123: modification time in rfc1123 (used in http)
  • modified_iso: modification time in ISO8601.
  • size: the size of file in bytes.

If the file is being translated (status=P)

  • ttime: the time the file started to translate

If the file is waiting in queue to be translated (status=Q)

  • qtime: the when the file was queued

If the file was translated (status=T,V,E,W,P,Q):

  • errors:number of errors in translation.
  • warnings: number of warnings in translation.
  • version: ClioInput version string
  • translated: the time of the last translation as a float
  • translated_string: S is the time of last translation in format “day-month-year hour-minutes”
  • rpt_url: is the URL to fetch the translation report
  • xml_url: is the URL to fetch the xml file
  • more_url: is the URL to fetch a properties file with extra info about the source

Parameters:

  • path (in the url): path to the directory
  • recurse=yes|no, recurse into the subdirectories of path

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

None

PARAMS
id
{{request_id}}

None

recurse
yes

None

Example Request
  • translations_get json output
  • translations_get text output
                                                
GET http://localhost:8089/rest/translations?id=&recurse=yes
Example Response

ids:
DELETE translations_delete
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/translations/git/mhk-sources/soure/soure-sources/sources/soure_fase1/notariais?id={{request_id}}&recurse=yes

Returns the translation status of a source and various metadata

Info returned for every file (extension .cli or .kleio in the path)

  • name: the name of the file in File, without the path.
  • path: the full path to the file.

  • status: T,V,E,W,P,Q if more than one apply the priority is P

    • T=needs translation
    • V=valid translation (can be imported)
    • E=translated with errors
    • W=translated with warnings
    • Q=file is in queue for translation
    • P=file is currently being translated

  • modified: the time of last modification , as a float

  • modified_string: the formated time of last modification using format ‘%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S’
  • modified_rfc1123: modification time in rfc1123 (used in http)
  • modified_iso: modification time in ISO8601.
  • size: the size of file in bytes.

If the file is being translated (status=P)

  • ttime: the time the file started to translate

If the file is waiting in queue to be translated (status=Q)

  • qtime: the when the file was queued

If the file was translated (status=T,V,E,W,P,Q):

  • errors:number of errors in translation.
  • warnings: number of warnings in translation.
  • version: ClioInput version string
  • translated: the time of the last translation as a float
  • translated_string: S is the time of last translation in format “day-month-year hour-minutes”
  • rpt_url: is the URL to fetch the translation report
  • xml_url: is the URL to fetch the xml file
  • more_url: is the URL to fetch a properties file with extra info about the source

Parameters:

  • path (in the url): path to the directory
  • recurse=yes|no, recurse into the subdirectories of path

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

None

PARAMS
id
{{request_id}}

None

recurse
yes

None

Example Request
  • translations_get text output
  • translations_get json output
                                                
GET http://localhost:8089/rest/translations?id=&recurse=yes
Example Response
200 - OK

GET versions_get_status_global
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/versions/status/global/?id=1234&recurse=yes&compare_to_branch=upstream/master

Gets information on the git repository associated with the sources.

The path after “versions” must start with a prefix that determines the type of information collected.

  • {Endpoint}/rest/versions/status/global[/path]
    • Gets an overview of the global status of the local branch, including divergence from origin and local change. The information is designed to provide an overview of what is going on in the remote and compare with local
      using logs and diff list.
    • The comparison is made between the current branch and origin. If another branch or remote is desired as trget it can be specified with the parameter compare_to_branch e.g. {Endpoint}/rest/versions/status/global[/path]?compare_to_branch=upstream/master.
    • It is possible to specify a local path after the prefix {Endpoint}/rest/versions/status/global/baptisms/1650 but the result will always refer to the whole branch to which the directory is associated as if git status was issued at the root of the git repository.
  • {Endpoint}/rest/versions/remote/branches[/path]
    • Gets information on the branches of the remotes associated to the repository of Directory. Works with information of the last fetch.For each remote branch gathers the following information: Name, commits ahead of current branch, commits behind, info on remote (name, origin, url).

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

Prefer json output

PARAMS
id
1234

None

recurse
yes

recurse into subdirectories (yes/no)

compare_to_branch
upstream/master

None

Example Request
  • versions_get_status_global comparing to upstream master
                                                
GET http://localhost:8089/rest/versions/status/global/?id=1234&recurse=yes&compare_to_branch=upstream/master
Example Response
200 - OK 
                                                    
Repository status: comparing "master" with "upstream/master" local time: 2020-08-19 16:10:51
Current dir: /Users/jrc/mhk-home/sources/api_tests/. Git root: /Users/jrc/mhk-home/sources/api_tests/ 
Current branch "master" is 16 behind and 4 ahead of "upstream/master"

Remotes:
  origin https://github.com/Timelink-project/soure-fontes.git (fetch)
  origin https://github.com/Timelink-project/soure-fontes.git (push)
  upstream https://github.com/joaquimrcarvalho/soure-fontes.git (fetch)
  upstream https://github.com/joaquimrcarvalho/soure-fontes.git (push)

PUT versions_put_pull
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/versions/pull/?id=1234

Calls the git pull command

Format: {Endpoint}/rest/versions/pull/path[?[parameters]]

Accepts the following parameters:

  • git_params = Options to be passed to the git command. This can be a string with options separated by spaces.
  • stash_before = if yes a stash push command will be done before the pull to avoid conflicts with current files

Returns:

  • output: output from git pull command
  • error: error from the git command if any.

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

Prefer json output

PARAMS
id
1234

None

Example Request
  • versions_put_pull (simple)
                                                
PUT http://localhost:8089/rest/versions/pull/?id=1234
Example Response
200 - OK 
                                                    
output=[Already up to date.]
error=[]
PUT versions_put_pull upstream
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/versions/pull/?id=1234&git_params=upstream/origin

Calls the git pull command

Format: {Endpoint}/rest/versions/pull/path[?[parameters]]

Accepts the following parameters:

  • git_params = More Parameters to be passed to the git command
  • stash_before = if yes a stash push command will be done before the pull to avoid conflicts with current files

Returns:

  • output: output from git pull command
  • error: error from the git command if any.

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

Prefer json output

PARAMS
id
1234

None

git_params
upstream/origin

None

Example Request
  • versions_put_pull (simple)
                                                
PUT http://localhost:8089/rest/versions/pull/?id=1234
Example Response
200 - OK 
                                                    
output=[Already up to date.]
error=[]
GET versions_get_remote_branches
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/versions/remotes/branches?id=1234&compare_to_brach=upstream

Gets information on the git repository associated with the sources.

The path after “versions” must start with a prefix that determines the type of information collected.

  • {Endpoint}/rest/version/status/global[/path]
    • Gets an overview of the global status of the local branch, including divergence from origin and local change. The information is designed to provide an overview of what is going on in the remote and compare with local
      using logs and diff list.
    • It is possible to specify a local path after the prefix {Endpoint}/rest/version/status/global/baptisms/1650 but the result will always refer to the whole branch to which the directory is associated as if git status was issued at the root of the git repository.
  • {Endpoint}/rest/version/remote/branches[/path]
    • Gets information on the branches of the remotes associated to the repository of Directory. Works with information of the last fetch.For each remote branch gathers the following information: Name, commits ahead of current branch, commits behind, info on remote (name, origin, url).

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

Prefer json output

PARAMS
id
1234

None

recurse
yes

recurse into subdirectories (yes/no)

compare_to_brach
upstream

None

Example Request
  • versions_get_remote_branches
                                                
GET http://localhost:8089/rest/versions/remotes/branches?id=1234&compare_to_brach=upstream
GET identifications_get_file
http://{{endpoint}}/rest/identifications/identifications/mhk_identification.json

Get identification files.

Identification files are json files containing identification of people and other entities.

Params: * path: if path points to a file, the content of the file is retrieved, if it is a directory the list of files in the directory are returned. If absent the source directory associated with the token is used. * recurse: if yes and the path is a directory, it will recurse into subdirectories.

HEADERS
Accept
application/json

None

Example Request
  • Sources get file (json output)
  • Sources Get File
